Ok now I have a totally different ask.  Russia has been banned from FIS events since 2022 and have been competing on their Russian Cup.

Here is my goal: Create a russia_scrape.py that works like all_scrape.py except that it gets results from https://flgr-results.ru/results?season=2026 where 2026 can be substituted with the year.  

In addition to changing how the HTML is scraped, we also need to translate things into English and fuzzy match names to match what I have on my systems.  

Here is the layout of scraping.  On the main results page you get a schedule for the season.

</html>
.  There are columns for Date, Competition, Category, Men and Women (from Google Translate).  Like the scrape.py, we want to mark the URLs of these pages so that they can be scraped from there.


When we click on those we get the results page we're looking for.  From this page we can extract everything we want to like we do in scrape.py.  

Date: </use></svg></span> 28.04.2018
City: {id:t,city:"г. Кировск"
Nation: Always will be Russia
Sex: {id:e,name:"Женщины",name_short:"Ж"}, but should be M for men and L for women
Distance: {id:E,name:"10 км СВ МСТ"
Technique: {id:E,name:"10 км СВ МСТ" (not sure what would be classic (C), freestyle (F))
Results" class="table-link">ДАВЫДЕНКОВА Мария</a></td><td style="text-align:center;">1992</td><td style="text-align:center;"><span class="app-table__classification">мсмк</span></td><td>Московская область</td><td style="text-align:center;">27:50.0</td><td style="text-align:center;">-</td><td style="text-align:center;">41.50</td></tr><tr data-row-key="431042" class="ant-table-row ant-table-row-level-0"><td colSpan="1" style="text-align:center;">2</td><td style="text-align:center;">5</td><td style="text-align:center;">200371</td><td><a href="/athletes/200371/" class="table-link">БЕЛАЯ Анна

Look something like this.  Doesn't seem like there's a place in it, so it place will need to be added on and the names will need to be romanized.  Let's make note of the ID (200371 for this athlete) and birth year (1992 for this athlete), so that when we match name and birthyear between the Russian dataset and the all_scrape dataset we can create a dictionary between the two.  

Event: <h1><span>Всероссийские соревнования</span>

The final csv should be similar to the one we make for all_scrape.py so minimal work needs to be done.  

So the columns should be,
Date in YYYY-MM-DD format
City: City
Country: Country
Sex: M or L
Distance: Distance (Спринт will be sprint), Эстафета will be Rel and Командный спринт will be Team Sprint
Event: Event
MS: 1/0 МСТ will be Mass Start
Technique: F, C, or P.  From what I can tell СВ is Freestyle, КЛ is Classic, Персьют is Pursuit
Place: Place
Skier: Romanized name that is fuzzy matched with the local version.  Remember the scraped version will be LASTNAME Firstname, so we need to make it Firstname Lastname and fuzzy match it.
Nation: Russia
ID: The ID from the local version if possible, otherwise the Russian one
Season: Season
Race: Race
Birthday: The version from local if possible, otherwise same format as the scrape.py shows but with the birthday being January 1 of the year since our scrape can't get the year
Age: Computed the same way
Exp: Computed like scrape.py

Other notes: We want to skip qualifications and roller ski races.  Квал wil lbe qualification and rollerski races which contains Лыжероллеры (or look like <a href="/results/2252/8895">ЛР - 20 км СВ< in the season page) should be skipped.
